Circumcision is not dismemberment of continuation like the other wounds; nevertheless, when we do this work of our own will and properly on children, it is necessary for us to do the best work, and the lightest for salvation.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not tell of their children's circumcision because they did not use it in their law, and we have nothing on this subject except what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor .i. dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule; si fuioit li keurs car il i a .ij. toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	For I have seen the greater part of masters and doctors who performed circumcision around the glans, and on strong ones, and on all a new foreskin; so the foreskin shrinks because there are two membranes, and by chance one grows above and the other below remains.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre; et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	Then they heal, and the pain is doubled, and in the healing which is from the nail there is no certainty that the point of the member is healed; and in the healing of the nail sometimes the iron slips away, and they ruin the work, and many times they heal in such a way that they do not need to be healed, and I have seen it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the healing that is done with strength throughout all the thread of the wound I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the forces cut justly above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en .i. tout soul tens; mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir; et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	Because when you press your hand, you cut evenly throughout all the threads of the wound; but let the thread be well tied around the skin, and let the manner of the first work be that you make the child think, if he understands, that you are only tying the thread around the rod, and then let him pull it in all the ways that he can.
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens; puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens; puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz .i. poc a .i. autre liien; et la tien as .ij. dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les .ij. liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	Then hold the rod straight between your hands, and stretch out the threads between your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see them, or any of the tools; then bind your hand to the rod and breathe on it, and draw it up so that the head of the rod is inside; then cleanse it well of the dirt that has gathered there, then tie the wound with a double thread, then tie it under another knot; and hold it for two days by the second ligature at the wrist and at the index finger, and press between the two knots, then lift the skin gently and draw out the head of the rod;
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres; et met poudre sus et sus la poudre .i. drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then let the blood run a little at a time, for that is the wound; and put powder on top of the powder, in a bandage glued with white of egg cooked and tempered with rosewater, confited with good and fresh rose oil, and leave it until the next day, and treat it with another treatment until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The form of the force for purification is as follows: the two knees should be relaxed and straight, and the hands should be as large as the forearm equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision; donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme; et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	The error of purification is when the wound inside bleeds; therefore, you should stretch it with your fingernail, so that the blood makes an abscess; then, press it equally, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, hold it with tweezers, and then press.
Et s’il trespassent .iij. jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement; si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	And if it bleeds for three days, and what is under the skin is swollen, let it be until the abscess is healed and the wound slightly scarred; then press as much as you can, and beware of the part of the penis, it will not harm him in any way.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point; cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Thus treat the site of sudden wounds with powder, as we said in the treatise on powders, and if it bleeds profusely and goes above, it will do no harm; therefore treat it, as we said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	retaining urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to stone, or frozen blood, or bowel, or dead fetus, or similar conditions, which we discussed in the previous sections.
et se li urine n’est desliie, et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	And if the urine is not released, and you see that it is retained due to a stone lodged in the neck of the bladder, then the patient should bend over his knees, with his feet placed on his back, stretching his abdomen from above the back, and restraining himself as much as he can. This compresses the neck of the bladder from above, forcing the stone to be expelled upward and releasing the urine.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	and if it does not come as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer extraction using an instrument called a "syringe". Its shape should be: made of thin silver, light like the feather of a bird; the cane should be a palm and a half in length, with a fine tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren .i. fil double, et lie au chief .i. poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	And the method of urination is to take a double thread, and tie a small ball of wool or cotton at the end, and insert the tip of the thread into the syringe; then squeeze out the excess wool and insert it into the syringe, then anoint the syringe with oil or butter and egg yolk, and have the patient sit on a chair, and lubricate the bladder and penis with moist oil, olive oil, and warm water.
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the body; then push the syringe forward until it reaches the bladder, and the patient will feel the urine flow into the void, and if this is not done according to this order, then the person guiding the syringe is doing it incorrectly. Then pull out the thread along with the woolen ball, and let the urine flow;
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and restart the syringe until the bladder is emptied and the patient is relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	of diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When blood or scabs appear in the bladder, and pus has gathered there, and you see water and medicine dripping, then use all the apparatus called a “clepsydra”, and that is its form:
Elle est close, et si a .iij. pertus: .ij. d’une part, et .i. d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	It is closed and has three openings: two on one side and one on the other, as you see; and the leather tube through which the medicine flows should be such that it blocks the penis without addition, so that one can squeeze out the moisture and push when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	and when you see your medicines enter the bladder, put the end of the syringe into the moisture and pull while squeezing the bulb; then release the bulb and push it in again; the moisture will enter the bladder immediately, and the patient will feel it.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	and this is the shape of the subtle catheter used to catheterize the bladder; it is like this:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a .i. sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les .ij. seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe .i. poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	And it is made of silver or bronze, and the head is larger; and under that there are two openings; then take a sheep's bladder and put in the fluid with which you want to catheterize the bladder, then tie the bladder between the two openings formed by a thin double string, and heat up the fluid on the fire; then insert the head of the catheter into the penis, then use your hand to push the fluid into the bladder until the patient feels that the fluid has reached the bladder.
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai .i. cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute .i. fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble .i. dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And if you don't have a bladder, take a piece of parchment, and make it into a circle, and pierce it all around; then thread a strong string through these holes, then assemble the circle like you would assemble a bag, and put inside what you want to use of oil and fluid and water, and tie it in the instrument; and do as you did with the bladder, pressing with your hand until the fluid reaches the bladder.
de la piere	of stones
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	We have already discussed in the division the methods of stones, and their extraction along with medicines; and I have described the difference between stones formed in the kidneys, and all the signs, and on which type of stone one should operate by cutting; and in the bladder, and in the penis; and I will explain it clearly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	I say that the stone which is formed in the bladder occurs more frequently in children, and it is a sign that the water flows from the bladder similar to water in its subtlety; and it appears as a vein, and the patient feels pain in his penis, and he can urinate many times, and then it swells; and most of these have stones at the bottom; and the treatment is easier for those who have large stones than for those with small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines. Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	And when we come to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient through a clyster, in order to draw out all the feces which are in the intestines. For they sometimes obstruct the retrieval of the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche ded ens;	Then take the patient by the feet and lift him up and move him from side to side so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it comes out from the upper part; then make him sit between your hands which are prepared with an apparatus, and his hands are underneath his thighs, so that the bladder is completely inclined downward; then you can feel for and touch it inside him;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere. Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	If you feel the stone in the bladder, then cut into the bladder. And if it does not move at all on touch, then moisten your left index finger with oil, if the patient is male, or your middle finger, if the patient is a young man; and insert it into the urethra, and seek out the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, draw it up to the neck of the bladder; then press in with your finger, and push the stone out where you see fit to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And instruct the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and instruct the patient to extend his testicles upwards in his right hand, and with his left hand pull back the skin under the testicles in the area where the incision is made; then insert the spatulum tightly, following its natural shape.
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	And cut between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the scrotum; and let it be straight over the stone, and your fingers pressed against the anus, and let the incision be across so that it is wide on top and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large;
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	by chance the pressure of the fingers against the anus may cause it to jump out without effort; and know that there is such a stone with angles and edges: if it is gritty, it will be easy to remove; and there is also one which is beneath, similar to a grape, and round, whose removal is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li .i. estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge .i. poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	In those therefore where it has angles and margin, make the incision larger; and if it does not yield, then you must use tweezers which are like a file at the end, to extract the stone so that it does not slip; or insert under it a very thin instrument bent at the tip; and if you cannot manipulate it thus, then enlarge the opening a little, and if the blood flows out, then stop it with vitriol.
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors. Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie. Car .ij. choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	And if there is more than one stone, then first insert the largest into the neck of the bladder, then press upwards, then draw it out, and the smaller ones after if there are several. And if it is very large, then split it, and make a larger incision. For two things can happen to the patient: he may die, or the urine may flow out through the opening that the urethra cannot heal; but in any case, try to draw it out, or break it up with tweezers, until you have extracted it in pieces.
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus .i. drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	And when you have finished your work, then pack the wound with incense, aloe, and dragon's blood, and hold it there, and place a wet cloth on top soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rosewater and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess; then resow the patient up his neck, and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen it, then wash the area very well with oil and water, then treat the wound with thin ointment and thick ointment, until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	And if hot abscesses come into the wound and corrosions, and congealing of blood in the bladder, and it is retained by this, which is known in such a way that without salt with the urine: therefore press your finger into the wound, and extract that blood, for if it remains, then the bladder will be damaged and burst.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les .ij. cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And then raise the wound with vinegar and oil and salt, and aid it in every way that you know, until it is healed; and it is necessary that every hour that you treat it, that you tie the two thighs, and assemble the remedies on the spot.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure. Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	And if the stone is small, and it is in the passage of the penis, and stuck in, and the urine cannot pass; then treat it as I say above, that you cut it many times, is one excuse for cutting through this treatment. I have already proven it in such a way.Et s’il est de la grosseur d’une noix ou de un ouef, et qu’il soit en l’entree del’estomac, si qu’ele ne puet issir sus le passage;
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	And if it is the size of a walnut or an egg, and it is in the entrance to the stomach, so that it cannot pass through the passage; take a piece of iron according to this shape and have 3 angles fixed on a stick:
puis pren .i. fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge. Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	then take a thread and tie it around the urethra under the stone so that it cannot return to the bladder; then gently push the probe into the urethra until it reaches the stone; and slowly turn the probe in your hand inside the stone, until you can pierce the stone from another side; then urine will come at once, press your hand on what remains of the stone which is inside the urethra. It is soon broken, and jumps out with the urine, and the patient is cured.
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie .i. fil desoz la piere et .i. autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les .ij. liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, then tie a thread under the stone and another one above it, then push the urethra against the stone between the two threads, then pull it out, and untie the thread, and clean the congealed blood in the wound; and cure it until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of female stones
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It sometimes happens that a stone becomes stuck in women, and if it does, the cure is painful, and it is forbidden for three reasons: one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin; and the second is that one cannot find a skilled woman who reveals herself to midwives, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a.	The third way is that one might not be able to find a woman who is skilled in this art; and the fourth way is that the woman's stone is deeper than the man's, so one must make a deeper incision, and there is great fear associated with it.
Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier .i. caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And if one must examine a woman, one should take a midwife who is very skilled, and with great difficulty force her on, and if she cannot be forced, do not use a cast of fine mire; but present her with a wise woman's bath in the manner of women, or a woman who knows some of the art, and command her to do what you command regarding the examination of the stone.
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And be sure to check if the woman is a virgin: then she should push her finger into her vagina and look for the stone; and if she finds it, she should hold it under her finger, and he should command her to push her finger into the anus and press her left hand firmly on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	If she finds it, then she should move the stone from the entrance of the bladder gradually to the root of the thigh, so that the stone comes out; then press on the stone at the root of the thigh against the middle of the urethra, where the movement appears, and feel the stone in that place; and do not move the finger above or below the stone, and let the incision be small at first.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains. si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	then pour the wine into the wound at the waist, feel the stone, and make the wound sore enough that the stone may come out; and know that there are many kinds of stones: small ones, large ones, rough ones, smooth ones, long ones, round ones, and rainy ones (stones that have a watery consistency). Know their likenesses in order to know how they will come out.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	And if the blood flows, then apply ground vitriol and hold it there for an hour until the bleeding stops; then return to your task, until the stone is out. Have the instruments that I have described to you at hand to assist you in your work on humans.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the blood flows and it is an artery that has been cut, then apply the powder to the wound and constrict it with bandages and bandages, and don't stop doing this; leave the stone and don't pull on it at all, or the patient might die. Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the swelling has gone down, return to your task until the stone is out.
de hernie carnouse	of a fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	Ramice aquouse is nothing other than the gathering of moisture or white pus, which is located under the membrane of the testicles, which holds the egg; and it is called "syfac", and sometimes it is properly in the membrane of the egg, if one believes that there is another egg; and this occurs when the skin of the testicle between the white pus that we have mentioned.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this ramice is due to weakness that comes to the testicles, and that matter is spread out.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture has many colors: sometimes it is declining towards yellow, sometimes red, sometimes black, sometimes watery white, and it happens in various other ways.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, .i. poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognize this condition, for if it is in the white syphilis that we have described, then the abscesses are red, i.e., slightly long like the shape of an egg, and do not open the skin, for there is moisture all around it.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the skin itself, then the abscesses are red with part of an egg, and because of this one thinks it is another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if the moisture is between the skin and the white syphilis, then one feels it well. Therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, probe all around it, for the shape is as mentioned earlier.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this, then judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	And when we treat it with iron, the patient should be bled according to their strength and the fullness of their body; then he lies on his back, on something slightly raised, and many garments are laid beneath him;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des .ij. costelz dou keur des coions;	then he sits on his left side and instructs the assistant to sit on his right, and extends the arm to one of the two ribs of the heart;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	then take the lit spatulum and cut the skin of the breasts between them from the long side up to the nipple, and make the incision straight while slicing the skin of the breasts carefully according to your strength;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a .i. large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	then pierce the plain syringe with a large hole, and draw out all the water, and then put in your fingers, and let the syringe fill; and do not touch the heart of the breasts, but only the syringe; cut all around it carefully, for if you do not cut it well, the water will return;
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les .ij. leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if the wound jumps out of place during your work, then reset it in its place when you have finished the operation; then sew together the two lips of the wound with a single stitch, and then treat it as you would any other wound until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the wound corrupted by another disease, then you should ligature the vessels that are suspended, fearing the flow of blood; then cut the skin all around the suspended area, extract the wound, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en .ij. parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont .ij. ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	And if pus is collected in two parts together, know that they are two abscesses; then cut the other part just as you did the first equally, then wash the blood away and put soft lamb's wool in oil into the wound.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les .ij. coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and put another piece of lamb's wool in wine and oil, and place it over the two wounds, and put on top double cloths, and tie it all around according to this form:
Puis pren .ij. drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les .ij. angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	Then take two pieces of cloth and stuff them with wool according to this shape, and sew them together at the crotch of the breeches, and let one piece cover the buttocks up to the back, and the other cover the front of the groin, and the remaining two pieces over the two sides, and tie it all tightly around the belt loop of the breeches.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes .i. cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	And sometimes this cloth cautery is used instead of an iron implement, and you should hold a small knife-like cautery gently against the skin of the testicles, and heat it as we have described, so that the white substance containing the water is revealed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Take the cautery according to this shape and pierce the testicle with it, and burn it with this fine hot cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	And scrape it in every way you can, until you extract everything; and be careful that the fire does not touch the egg; and know that this method is safer; and beware of bloodletting and the dangers of cutting.
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if nothing contradicts you, then treat any abscess, bleeding, or other condition according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai,	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this procedure due to its horror, then perform a perforation as I have told you, and when you are certain through the signs that we have discussed that the pus is drained,
si fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege leveit; puis perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	have the patient sit on a high seat; then pierce the abscess at its lowest point to the depth of a finger's breadth, and insert the probe deeply into the body; make the holes large enough so that all the pus can flow out;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then place cotton on the wound and bind it, and leave it to drain the remaining pus, then treat the wound until it is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge .i. poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés .vj. mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and if the white membrane does not allow the water to exit through the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a tube or instrument used to treat dropsy, as described earlier; and open the wound slightly, and let the water flow out, and it will accumulate again after six months or so, and when it has accumulated as before, then the patient's days are numbered.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicle abscess
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in this branch of medicine, there are many dangerous dispositions, and therefore I believe it is better to leave it alone.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you about the procedure and what the abscess should look like.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	I therefore say that many abscesses come about in the body, especially in the testes; and this happens in many cases.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is due to an abundance of sour and bitter humours, which are spread to the testes, or from a blow;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and the colour of the abscess follows the colour of the body; and it does not cause pain, and is a serious abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and sometimes there are grey, purulent, and pus-filled abscesses, and sometimes they come from a burst artery, or inflammation of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is a burst artery, it is known by the warmth of the abscess when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and you must not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois,	That which is caused by vein inflammation is known through its appearance when pressed with the fingers,
et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	and one can properly make an incision based on this appearance, and on other characteristics;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and you cup the heart of the testicles, then they rise up, and the thread comes out from under the white sac, and free the suspensory ligament all around the testicle.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the testicle is already swollen with these new bumps, then you must therefore draw out the testicle and cup it;
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	and if it is swollen in the sac, or in what is inside the vessels, then you must release all that tension and cup it smoothly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the swelling is in the rear location, then you must cup it all and extract the testicle, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is finished, then cover the wound with soft wool moistened in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a .i. borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions,	This is an abscess wrapped in a wrapper similar to .i. bud, with the softening of the testicles,
et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	and the patient feels great pain when he walks;
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant,	and the treatment for this illness is just as difficult as the one described above.
et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	Nevertheless, we will tell you about its treatment according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus .i. siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois,	You should make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then tie the suspensory of testicles tightly with your fingers,
a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	as well as all the vessels that are near the penis, and grab them firmly, and stretch them forcefully;
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert,	then cut wide through the vessels with a spatula, so that they are exposed,
et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	and then scorch from each side, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries which are in the temples;
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	then he inserts a needle where there is .a. double thread, and ties it at the first place where the screw came out, and ties it directly to the other end;
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	then he cuts them straight through the middle, according to the length of the body, and draws out the corrupted moisture;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	then treat the wound as with the others, except we bind it tightly, so that no blood vessels burst to either side;
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	for in this way no harm comes from it, and if all the vessels are empty, one must milk out the testicles through all the vessels;
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the vein does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and they dry out and cannot help themselves.
de la routure dou syfac	from the rupture of the sinus
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The causes of this disease are either the rupture that leads to syphilis, or the swelling on the abdomen in the region of the intestines, causing them to descend from their normal location into one of the groins.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces .ij. manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	This rupture can be caused by two things: either from a punch or kick, or from lifting a heavy object, and similar actions.
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	The signs that it is caused by the swelling of syphilis are that it happens gradually over a long period of time, and does not occur suddenly.
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	And the abscesses are even throughout, pressing on the intestines because of the swelling.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are that it is of the section of the syphilis, that it causes sudden pain at the beginning, and there are various abscesses appearing beneath the skin, close to the surface, and this is due to the escape of the intestines and the body from the syphilis.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the intestines descend with the feces, and are held back, causing great pain to the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these treatments of iron, there is fear, because of which one should abstain.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the method of the treatment is that you command the patient to draw in his intestines with his hand inside the wound, if he can return them;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then let him sleep on his back, between your hands, and gently lift his legs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then they stretch the skin of the scrotum upwards, and cut all around the testicles;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then put in the probes into the groin according to what you need to open the wound, and let it be such that the blood can flow out;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then cut off the foreskin under the skin of the scrotum, as much as the white foreskin is hard all around;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac,	then put your index finger into the opening of the scrotum, in between the white membrane which is under the testicle skin, and between the second membrane.
et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and push the testicle towards the scrotum with your left hand, and hold the white membrane taut upwards in your right hand, and lift the testicle out of its sac towards the body;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the assistant to stretch the testicle upwards, and loosen what is tight behind the sac;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and feel with your fingers if there is any wrapped intestine or tough white membrane, and if you find anything, put it back into the abdomen;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait .i. gros fil fait de .x. filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait .iiij. filz;	then take a needle with .1. thick thread made of .10. threads, and pierce the posterior part of the scrotum, which is after the skin of the testicles; after the scrotum, then tie the threads that appear, so that there are .4. threads;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de .ij. pars;	then tie them one above the other in the manner of a cross, and tie the scrotum, which we said was under the skin of the testicles, with a strong thread of .2. parts;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de .ij. pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then wrap the threads around the scrotum and tie them tightly at .2. parts, so that none of the veins that nourish it can enter, lest an abscess form there;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc .ij. dois de celui, et aprés ces .ij. liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and put the thread according to the first long line .2. fingers from that one, and after these .2. lines leave the scrotum which is under the skin of the testicles the width of a finger;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	and after all the others according to the roundness that the egg carries; then cup in the part which is under the skin of the testicles, as far as the blood flows, and the bowel, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then administer wool moistened in oil, and place it on the wounds, and then administer the ligature that we have described.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white syphilis that we have described is cauterized after the incision, out of fear of bloodletting.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	For it happens many times, and let the ligature stay on until it bleeds; and if it is slow to bleed, then use hot water, and put on what we have said, until it bleeds.Et s’il ne peut cheoir, si doit être incisez sus la piere, selonc que li semblet a voire, et laine moillie en oile, et liien, si com nos avons dit ci devant.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another treatment until it is completely healed.
de hernie carnouse	of a fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone dare to perform the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is performed like the ramifica that is together with the vein, in such a way that you ligature the vessels, after the incision gently from above downward;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then bandage me tightly, and lance the abscess of the one who opens it, until the vessels burst; and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	Sometimes there is internal bleeding, as we have said, and the opening appears; and none of the intestines come out into the rectum, and if any do, it is a little, and they heal quickly.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	However, if he stays too long in this position, the wound or fistula will become infected, causing the intestines to protrude.et se leu est grand et large, et les intestins pendent, si covient il que tu remettes li cuitel en son leu sus l’estomac, et tu tiens li cuitel si fort que tu puisses,
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	And this happens due to the extension of the fistula in the intestines, as we have said, for it is stretched, then softened and swollen, and the opening appears;et se li intestins sont en dan, si covient il que tu trusses li cuitel de touts costez, si fort que tu puisses.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and the treatment if it is by cautery, as we have said before; and sometimes it is treated with iron in this way:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de .iij. dois;	and the patient lies on his back between your hands, then press the location of the rupture gently with the tip of a large needle according to the size of three beans;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	then pull out the skin tag underneath the skin and take a piece of rag and put it over the visible skin tag;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les .ij. leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	then press on the stomach, then cut the two locations on the skin tag on the head of the rag, and cut one and the other;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then pull out the head of the vein and do not cover it with syrup or stretch the udder or anything else, as I have informed you in the treatment of the rupture of the intestines;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies. Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	then treat it with the treatment of wounds. And when you cut the threads, clean and treat the wound until it heals.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	Syrup is constricting and has no appearance in a hernia, and cauterization is beneficial in this case, and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the scrotum
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin of the testicles becomes soft in some men, because the parts within are softened, and it appears milky white; and when one wishes to treat it, he should have the patient lie on his back, and cut away the skin which is softened above the natural skin; then bring together the two lips with a single stitch, and if you see fit, sew the superfluous soft skin with three or four stitches firmly; then cut between the stitches, and treat it as other wounds until it is healed, and remove the thread.
dou chastrement	of castration
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por .ij. manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes. Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc .ij. manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.  En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.  Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a .i. cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	You should know that castration is prohibited in our law, and because of this, I would rather not discuss it in this book. It is only necessary for two reasons: one is so that the veterinarians can respond when asked, and know how to treat [the animals]; the other is because we often need castration to help certain beasts, such as bulls, rams, horses, and other animals. I say then that castration is done in two ways: by attraction or by cutting. In the method of castration by attraction, you make the animal sit in warm water until the testicles are softened and hanging; then grab them with your hand and squeeze until they are removed and you no longer feel anything. As for castration by cutting: you should tie the animal down, and cut the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then cut each sac at one cut, when you have well scalded them; I leave some pus and the thin membrane that covers the vessels; this method of castration is better than the one by attraction, because in the one by attraction, something from the testicles may remain, which causes the animal to desire sexual intercourse; then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc .ij. manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les .ij. coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.  Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et .ij. coions.  Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	Hermaphrodites are of two kinds: one like men in that between their legs there is an aperture like a woman's, with pubic hair, and sometimes they urinate from it; the other kind is like women, having a small penis on the underside of their scrotum and two testicles. In both cases, treat them as you would any other patient; for those who are more like men, where the urine flows from the skin between their testicles, there is no treatment.
de la tentigene	of the testicles
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure. Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee». Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	Tentigen is an abscess on the natural part, so disfigured that it is painful to look at; some women have it as large as a hand, and this is the cure. You must paint over the excess of the tentigen with your hand or fingernails, and scrape it gently; do not press too hard, lest bleeding ensue, then cure one disease with another until it is healed. There is also an abscess that emerges from the mouth of the uterus, resembling a cow's udder, and for this reason they call it 'cow disease'. You should scrape it as you would the tentigen, as we have said, and cure it until it is healed.
de erratique	of Errata
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile. Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait. S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as .ij. leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes .ij. dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les .ij. leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder. Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte. Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.  Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez. Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	An errata is when the nature of the woman is not understood, or the passage is narrow; and it can be due to genetics from birth, or an accident from illness that came later; or it could be caused by a foreign object, or a thin or thick discharge, and is made deep within the vagina, or on the sides, or lower down, wherever it may be; and they should be examined during conception and childbirth, and perhaps during flowering as well. Knowledge of this comes from observing the dance. If the discharge is apparent nearby, either between your fingers or close to the vagina, then act quickly: place your two fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread apart; then form a seal with your fingers so that the thin discharge is stopped, and cover the discharge with wool soaked in oil. Then have the woman lie down for several days so that it does not heal over. If the discharge is thick and hard, you should treat it similarly to a spasm like one would with a myrrh leaf. If the discharge is from an abscess, then it should be treated by soaking in vinegar and then covered; and have at hand medicines that stanch blood, such as acacia, dragon's blood, incense, and egg white; then insert a large piece of clean linen so that the wound does not heal over; and keep it this way for a long time, and use other treatments until it is healed. And when there is a discharge from an abscess in the vagina, one should not touch it to treat it.
des emorroides	of Hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation. Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer. Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer. Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses; puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai .i. emplaustre sus son dos. Et se il estainche, c’est boin. Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir; puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.  Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a .i. chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Hemorrhoids are opened veins from which blood flows incessantly, and when they are old, they become thrombosed; and we have already described their appearances, signs, and treatments in a previous section. I will now describe those that can be cured. When hemorrhoids or thrombosed veins are completely out of control and no longer respond to treatment, then one must use cauterization with hot iron. Those that can be felt at the edge of the anus can be treated, but those that are deeper cannot. First, the patient should be placed in a cool room, then the hemorrhoids should be tightened with ligatures, and their roots should be cut, followed by the application of powder made from astringent medications such as acacia, dragon's blood, and incense. Then, the feet should be immersed in cold water for an hour, and if there is any bleeding, the patient should be bathed in a decoction of sumac, pomegranate bark, galls, and similar ingredients. Then, take barley flour, mix it with honey and garlic, and apply it as a poultice to the back. If the bleeding stops, that's good. If not, use leeches on the back and breasts without using iron; then take woolen cloth, soak it in plantain juice or dogwood bark infusions with old wine, and apply it to the affected area. When the abscess has drained, treat the wound with ointments until it heals completely; and if there is one called "albathir", which is red and resembles a rough patch, it should be covered as I have described for thrombosed veins, and then treated until it heals completely.
des apostemes de la marris	Here is the translation of the next sentence:
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division. Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe; et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.  Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie; et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus .i. siege, et ait .ij. petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe; et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien; puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme; et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide; et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve; et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument. Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit; et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec; et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites; puis le cure aprés .ij. jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez; et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites; puis reveigne a l’oignement.  Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	Here is the translation:
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar: adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir; adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui; et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost; car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification; et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment. Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises; si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	It is necessary for the midwife to first know the natural shape of childbirth and its signs: when you see a woman struggling to go down, and desiring to smell aromatics; then the child hastens to come out; then you know that this childbirth is according to nature, and the afterbirth comes out with it, and the mother's superfluities are cleansed by good purification; and those who come in other ways do not come naturally. For sometimes they come on their feet, and come out of the body or the shoulder, and the hands, or they come on their stomach, or back, and are accidentally turned onto their neck, and in many other bad shapes; so it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and cunning in these matters, and beware of errors and deceptions, and I will show you all the shapes and how one should help them.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent; et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	If the child comes out on its head by natural delivery, and the woman gives birth painfully, and her strength is weak, then make her sit on a chair or have women hold her; and give the midwife a small sponge soaked in rose oil or fried fenugreek between her fingers, and then insert it into the child's mouth:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers; et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament; puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre: si istra maintenant l’enfes.Et se les .ij. mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc; et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus .i. siege, et li lieve les piés en haut; puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement; et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and split the afterbirth, and squeeze its nail until the moisture that is inside flows out; and press the mother's belly so that the child descends, and if it does not descend, then the woman must be enema with a fenugreek mucilage of sisamen oil; then make her sneeze and cough up phlegm, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour: then the child will come out. And if both hands come out, then you must gently pull them back little by little; and if they cannot enter, then put the woman on a chair, and lift her feet up; then stand the chair on the ground, and make the woman defecate so that she does not strain while standing; and if the hands cannot enter, and the child dies, then grip the hands at the knuckle that is placed in front as mentioned earlier, and pull out the child, and reset it in the same way.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piez	of the birth of the child on its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child is born on its feet, it should be turned upside down.
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	And then turn it slowly and gently until it is straight;
puis preigne .i. des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then grasp one of the feet and stretch it out slowly.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When it jumps up to the armpit, instruct it to catch, and make it sneeze with scent.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	if it jumps out, God willing.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not jump out as we have said, then pull it back little by little, until it is in its natural position.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it will be easy.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons dit, si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en .i. mortier;	And if it does not come out as we have said, then take musk, and oil of vitriol, and melted gum, and grind everything in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement,	and apply this ointment to the nature of the woman inside and out
puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	then have her sit in warm water up to her ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai .i. coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is soaked underneath, make her a collar of myrrh and put it on her, and leave it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then make her sit on a chair, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and gently press her belly, for the child will jump out now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	for the child to come out onto his knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this way, then put the midwife's hands on him little by little;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor .i. lit;	then let him be laid on his back, and let his feet hang down, and let him lie on a bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and bends his hands a little bit, then presses his hands on the belly, removing the cushions underneath so that it is exposed below.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not jump, he takes his feet and moves them around, then he moves his belly upwards, then he puts your hands in.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc; et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and rock the child gently; and instruct the woman to hold on until the child emerges.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the child's exit, which comes out wide a hand's breadth
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	We need to figure out how to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if we cannot bring it back, then make the woman stand up and walk.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus .i. lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	If she cannot walk, then make her lie on a bed and raise her legs straight;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then administer the medicine that I have described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, then have her sit on a chair, then study to bring the hand back;
