et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and turn the child according to its natural position, and make her sneeze, and command her to grip as the child emerges.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	from the emerging of the child onto its neck, and spread out his hands, and turn his face towards his mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	I want to grab her hand, then slowly turn it, and gently wiggle it;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is even, put on the muscle a poultice of honey and oil, as we have said, then instruct it to move little by little.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne; et la fai esternuer.	and when you have done this, make her sit on a chair, and instruct her to sneeze; and make her yawn.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same way for all of the secondine
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes out in this way for all of the secondine, then scrape the secondine at your fingernail, as long as the moisture is discharged.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the child lies on its face and neck, and the mother holds it back, it will not be restrained and the child will die;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then put the child inside, so that you have placed it as it should be, and command the woman to squeeze herself several times:
adonques si istra legierement.	then if she strains gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the issue of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent .iij. ou .iiij.; et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	Know that twins are born many times, and sometimes triplets or quadruplets; and this is not a strange thing, but happens rarely.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Twins are a strange thing, and do not live long if they are born too soon.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they are multiple, and are separated by the placenta which divides them, which is attached to the womb;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they are born just as naturally as one baby, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they are bleeding profusely, then the treatment as we have said, and the assistant should be skillful, and quickly and lightly perform what she does;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do thus as it is best for their health.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris .i. ou .ij. ou .iij. ou .iiij. ou .v. ou .vj. ou .vij., ou plusors jusc’a .xv., et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious,	Some are formed in the womb 1 or 2 or 3 or 4 or 5 or more up to 15, and are all formed in the shape of a child according to the measurement of the wise glorified.
et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	and the surgeon must know all this, for by chance a similar thing might happen to him;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	then he should act accordingly.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you are curing a woman of childbirth, as I have said in the previous chapter, and there is no progress, and you are forced to use manual intervention;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	if you must know whether the woman is of sound body, and has no accident or fear of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	the woman should be laid on her back, with her hips inclined downward, and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de .ij. pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the midwife should apply the ointment of .ii. parts, or she will be bound to the bed if the child is not delivered;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the mouth of the mother with moist oils mixed with alder and fenugreek and flax seed, then anoint the midwife's hands with these oils and musks;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere .i. leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu,	then gently tap them, then press them where they are convenient to this,
et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	and be careful that the infant is not equipped so that it descends upon its head;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez,	if he thrusts the fingernails into his own eyes or throat or mouth or palate or under the beard or near the ribs,
et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	and if the descent is on the feet, he should thrust or pinch and press the middle parts;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and he should dye the hair on his right hand, and place the cloth between the fingers of his left hand, and tie it tightly all around his hand, and insert the needle into any of the places we have mentioned, until he reaches the hollow;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the shape of the needle:
puis fiche encontre .i. autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then insert it against another needle, or a third one if you need more, so that the extractions are equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then they should be moved equally from one side to another, in order to move it out, and the needles should be bitten down to hold it in place, as shown in this illustration:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if some of it remains, then anoint the ball of one of his fingers with oil, and rub that part with it, and pull at the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if nothing remains, then put this joint higher up, and do this until it all comes out firmly.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement,	And if one hand comes before the other, and he cannot bring it back due to the dislocation,
si covient que tu envoloupes sus .i. drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	then you must wrap it up in a cloth, until it is fully extracted;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as .ij. piés.	then cut into the joint of the sole or the heel, and thus you must do to the other hand and foot.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee,	And if the head of the child is large and it is tight in the birth canal, or if it has an acute, gathered mass on its head,
si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	you must place the spiny spatum between your fingers, and open up the head and extract the fluid.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you can use the instrument called "almidach," of which the shape comes from the instruments or chapters that follow this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and so also naturally the fetus in the womb;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles,	and then pull out the bones with tongs,
et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and if the shoulder pops out and it is forced out, it should be split so that the moisture which is in the wound comes out;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, then cut it into pieces as much as you can;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, then you must pierce it so that the moisture runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is on his feet, the pulsing is light, and the pulse at the mouth of the wound is weak.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if there is swelling in his belly or his feet, then you must apply a hot compress wrapped around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and open the belly or the foot, so that the moisture which is inside runs out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	and if the other members are removed, and the head remains,
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	then he should put his hand into the wound and pull it up to the mouth of the wound;
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	then he should take a hook or two, and pull it out;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	and if the mouth of the wound is narrowed due to a hot abscess that has formed there, one should not work on it,
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	then one must administer moist and fatty things;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and apply poultices, and use hot water that is softening and moistening.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its back, and you can lay it flat, then administer what we have said for a living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one has no strength, then carry the body away in pieces, and leave nothing of the placenta.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, if he is affected with those abscesses that come in the sea,
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and bloodletting comes about, let it be placed in restraining water, and let him receive other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman whose fetus had been dead inside her belly; then another was sewn over it, and the other one died as well.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came in her armpit, and it swollen so much that it opened up and began to discharge profusely.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the cure, and I thought long and hard, but could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a strong attracting poultice, and out came a bone, and after a few days, some more.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very astonished, because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that they were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	I examined the wound and found bones beneath, until the woman was in a better state.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman walked like this for a long time, and then suddenly a little bit of blood came out from it.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I remember this chapter especially because when the masters find something unusual, they know how to treat it effectively.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring the dislocation back to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Hereafter comes the form of the press, with which one is equipped in books; and at two turns of the two sides of the two lines.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horns should be more subtle on the constrictor, and made of boxwood or ebony;
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the staves should be one digit wide, and the edges of the trees one digit apart, and their length a palm and a half;
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and in the two sides should be two ajustments of this same wood, which are firmed in one and the other, a half-palm long or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	and these two settings are put into the mouth of the wound to open it when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, its appearance more subtle and lighter, is made of ivory or boxwood, according to the appearance of tweezers;
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	and has two heads two settings, as you see, a palm long, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	and when you see to open the wound with all the instrument, then let the woman sit on a bed, her feet hanging and her legs spread,
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	then bind the two joints together in the marrow, and hold the head of the instrument under between his thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand along the instrument, just as you did with the forceps, according to the amount that you see the opening of the marrow, so that the operator does what he wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These instruments are all tapered and have multiplied their likenesses; and when the operator has prepared them, they are more nimble in their work and more effective for people due to their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despair of the instrument until you have prepared it, for their necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath, then make her sneeze using a condiment, and squeeze her hands to her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she vomits, all the better.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a pot and place herbs that can open the mouth of the mother, such as calming agent, rue, anise, chamomile, casia lignum, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All of these herbs, or some of them, are cooked in a pot over fire. Then put one end into the pot's spout and the other end into the mouth of the mother:
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	and the tinder until the smoke comes inside the wound; then make her sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	Then the scabs will fall off quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	And if it remains after this treatment and is not cured, then order the patient to soak her left hand in oil of sesamum or in a poultice of alder, and then wash it in the natural way.
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and she will find the scabs; and she should pick at them and pull them off bit by bit gently so that the wound is not hurt.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	but it must be moved slightly to the right and left, and then pulled; it will then come out and separate.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the wound is tight, we have described the treatment of sneezing, and the fuming of herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it does not become looser from all that we have said, then beware of pulling;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary for the one who is at the mouth of the wound to tie it to the woman's thigh, then cleanse it with an ointment of tetrafarmacon;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	if she vomits and expels it, and comes out; but nevertheless, when she vomits, it gives off a bad odor in the stomach and head, and weakens the illness.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	If this is the case, then suitable smoke treatments are needed: some of the ancients have tried smoke from watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one smokes out the woman is for the retention of flowers and secondine if it is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is made of glass, resembling a cane, and one puts the fine end in the nature, and the wide end above the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and there shall be smoke over the coals, and the mould until it is destroyed, and begin another.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born without their foundation being pierced, but instead have a thin, subtle membrane.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, the midwife should pierce this membrane with her finger, and not with a sharp instrument, and keep the baby from moving so that she does not touch it.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then put on warm wine and oil, then the ointment until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will heal, put a wooden peg in the hole and leave it for several days, then remove it when the child wants to go to bed.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And sometimes the clotting comes suddenly from a wound or abscess; then it must be covered suddenly: then it should be treated, as we have said, with a peg of wood.
de la fistule dou fondement	from the fistula in the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from under the anus are nodular and grow larger than those that originate in other parts of the rectum, or in the space between its two walls.
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	If there is one or more fistulas; and when that nodule becomes old, it opens up, and usually releases a white pus or thin fluid.
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And sometimes these fistulas are persistent; and they are caused by what comes out of the body through flatulence or emissions when the patient passes gas, and sometimes a little bit jumps out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And there are fistulas that pierce all the way to the bladder, and halfway down the shaft of the penis; and they can reach the hip joint, and the head of the thighbone.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the fistula, which seeps at the anus, and does not seep;
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you pierce your index finger or anus, and pierce a fine needle of bronze or iron into the fistula when there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has twisting, then pierce it with a thin tent of lead or a horsehair, until you feel the tent or hair in your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and it does not come out of the orifice with excretion or wind, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	Know that she does not pierce; then heal quickly.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula has reached the bladder or the urinary tract, and the urine flows out, and it cannot be stopped by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced up to the hip joint, then the tent is placed up to the spot.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no pain and the tent is removed, then it is healed without medicine or ointment.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and for these persian fistulas there is no treatment other than hard work and the folly of those who meddle in them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	In that which is not persian and is not old, there is hope of healing through iron, as I have experienced.
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and the patient lies on his back, and lifts his legs up to his hips, and has his hips tilted towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then insert a tent of iron, or of lead if there is tortuosity, as far as you know where the tent comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the pain is felt around the anus, you must insert your finger.
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	then feel if the tissue is piercing your finger; and if it is discovered where you feel it between your finger and the flesh, then know that it is piercing;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if you cannot work on it, it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One can still heal some, but it happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and if aid is given, one should heat the fine cautery according to the width of the fistula, as was said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and insert it into the fistula as far as the base; and do this .2 or .3 times, until you know that the burnt flesh, which resembles an owl feather, has been removed;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treat it with moist bandages soaked in butter until the dead flesh comes away, and then apply ointment to heal and seal the wound.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it is healed in this way, that is good. If not, then it cannot be healed otherwise;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent enters and does not pierce to the bone which is at the foundation, and between your finger and the tent there is a thick covering of flesh or skin, and you see the fistula following the covering down to the heart;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if you cut into the beginning of the fistula and push in the tent before it, and then cauterize after it, until it reaches the tip of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	and the tent will be released and fall out; then cut away those false meats that look like a bird's feather, and nothing will remain.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the pus flows out, and enters between you and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or a medicinal agent.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For fire cautery brings about two things: scorching of the flesh and stopping of blood and drying up moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then dress with tent-canvas moistened in butter or ground substances until the pus runs out and the flesh heals;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound with ointments of heating herbs that are dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes all the way from the fundament, and is separated from the body, put your finger in it or in the fundament, and explore inside.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the tent, and between them is the membrane or skin, or it is about to burst, then there are no forces that can stop it except through one of three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	either you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it all the way to the bottom, or if you can, put in tents and treat it as before.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep, lest you cut the lining that holds the fundament, and let the evacuations come out through there instead.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then cure, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance if it is healed, or you remove that covering and clean it once the ulcer is cut away from the bone, or with a sharp instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then probe the wound, as far as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	then examine the wound and seek to heal it, and keep the fistula in the part above the bone: if there is any lighter thing for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes there are fistulas according to this method: and it is when you push the tent into the fistula, and it is on the side of the foundation under the skin above.
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	take a tent pierced at the tip according to this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And he puts a twisted thread into 2, and puts the tent all the way through the thread into the fistula as far as the tip.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is piercing in the margin within the foundation, then pull out the thread from that hole, so that you put your finger on the foundation;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	And draw the head of the thread, and gather the two heads together, and squeeze one against the other, and let it be for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it sometimes, until the threads catch the hairs that are between them, and pull them out;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then dress the wound until it is healed and cleaned.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not open, then make it open in every way you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For one must not bandage it tightly for a long time, and then treat the wound as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spiny sputum, which one makes into a fistula, is very sharp and pointed on one side.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other side it is smooth, so that it should not be bandaged as it should not be, as you see here.
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Hemorrhoids are of two types: sometimes they are inside the anus, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones; they often cause blood to flow out.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	There is one or more of them, and some are outside the anus and some at its entrance; but those that are outside have less moisture.and are smaller:
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	and sometimes they discharge a little yellow water or a little blood, and their color is like that of the body;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those who have them inside the anus is that you instruct the patient to strain until they go out in a bowel movement, and then the hemorrhoids will come out;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you are in a hurry, and can't use tweezers, hold it with your fingernail, then grab it at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if they can't hold it due to moisture, then grab it with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of camel hair;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and pull them out with your fingers, then grab and twist them, and powder some hot powdered medicine on them that is in place of cauterization;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you can cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cauterization, then treat with other treatments until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundations cannot come out, then enema the patient with a sharp and rough enema to wash what is in the foundation, so that it can come out clearly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	if the patient defecates, and if the thread comes out of the anus, then the treatment is light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you should grab them with your fingernail or tweezers, and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed and no longer fear an incision with iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	If you need to do the sewing in this way: take a twisted thread and put it in a needle, then bring the two ends of the thread above the needle, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle,
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if it is too large; tightly pull the thread, then tie the thread, and remove the needle, and do likewise with all the others, and leave one to draw out the excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place on the wound a damp cloth moistened with rose oil or with cerate, and place it on the wound, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then leave them until they fall off, and when they have fallen off, treat the wounds with ointment and other treatments until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	from dryness of the penis or anus
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there is dryness of the bowels due to constipation, and because of the natural confinement, and when the illness is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	Then you should cut the skin at the tip of a spatula or your nail, so that it does not become moist.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then he should be bled until he is healthy, as is appropriate.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if he cannot become healthy, then the bleeding should be repeated more aggressively than before, until he is healed and bled;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat until healed.
dou fremit	where there is trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A flea is a small creature that moves quickly throughout the body,
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes it bites and can be felt like a trembling, and it affects the whole body, but especially the hands more than any other part.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a candle made of goose fat, or from the fat of a strong vulture, and place this candle on the wound, so that the purple circle encompasses the entire wound.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then return your hand to the candle and stroke all around the wound, pushing it in deeply and pulling out the wound from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see that it is made of an iron or steel candle according to this form, and it is subtle underneath and drawn above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	do not pierce it, so as to hold the wound, and to press it And if you see that the wound is cauterized, as in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Sometimes the enema is made of silver or brass, or molten copper or hammered; and sometimes they are made from these small and large instruments, according to those who use them.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those who administer treatment for children and the feeble and painful, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the enema, whether small or large, is placed above, or the abdomen is bound according to this method:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and has a protrusion where the belly is tied, as you see, and the intestines are pierced inside; and it has two openings on one side, and one on the other;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	and the belly where one puts the medicine is made of a beast's bladder or parchment, and it is pierced all around with small holes,
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and between each hole there is a distance of one digit, then tie into these holes a strong thread wound in a spiral around ten or so times, and assemble the belly like a goat;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument in front with a strong thread, then colonoscopy; and this is the shape of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	Let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and anoint the head of the syringe with oil or egg white, or a similar thing, then insert it gently.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then the minister squeezes it with his two hands together, until it is completely empty, then withdraws the syringe and leaves the patient's legs exposed,
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if the medicine wants to come out, let it leak as much as it can; and if he sleeps for a night afterward, it is even more helpful.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you syringe him for a disorder of descending stomach, and the medicine rushes out, then you repeat it until he is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are in the anus or rectum, then the enema should be as fine as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the subtle enema that stretches the skin:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have already discussed in the division the cure of wounds; now we will discuss manual and medicinal cures according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse depending on how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and by what they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things that make wounds are by the impact of stone, and cutting with sword or knife, or lance or staff, or arrow, or similar objects.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	Or they are made according to the parts of the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, or the head, or the leg, or the belly, or the liver, and similar members;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the cure for each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, because the recollection will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head, and the bone is not broken, one should take care if it is from a blow from a stone or similar object, and the skin is still broken and the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you suspect a hot abscess quickly: then let him bleed from the head itself if there is a little blood coming from the wound, and let the bleeding be in the opposite direction of the wounded part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and let the patient avoid excess wine and rich foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to bleed, then let his food be diminished, and let him not drink wine or eat meat;
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and place sorrel on the wound, if a hot abscess forms, use cotton wet only in rose oil, or in astringent wine;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if there is no hot abscess, place on the wound, if it is fresh and bleeding and has not been moved by the air, powder which I will describe a little later;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if the burn has been moved by the wind, then place on it some ointments until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large, like that of a sword cut and similar, and the lips cannot be closed with sutures, then close it by sewing it shut, as I will describe for abdominal wounds.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is exposed to the bone, and open, and only attached by a little, then cut it; then cure the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh in place of skin,
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	and instruct the patient to eat coarse foods like testicles and cooked wheat, as well as meat and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find rot in the skin, and it doesn't reach the bone, then cut off the rotten part completely, and then cure it;
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	and if there is an artery in the wound or vein, which bleeds profusely and cannot be staunched by medicine, then tie it off with a thread;
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	and if this does not help, then cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, the treatment is easy: you should put this powder on so that the burn has healed.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the way of making the powder is this: take incense one part, dragon's blood two parts, quicklime three parts, and ground it finely.
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	and apply it to the wound, and hold it firmly until it heals well and joins back together with its blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	bind it tightly, and leave it bound if it is not swollen, for one does not remove the bandage until the wound has healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes one applies chalk alone when one does not have incense or dragon's blood, but one should move the wound with the cautery.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the cautery has moved the wound, one should not put any of this powder on it;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but one should apply certain digested ointments, or poultices of barley flour made with water and honey, until it becomes soft;
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat other treatments until he is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the fracture comes with the wound, and it is small, then pull it out with fine tweezers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you later about fractures of the head.
de la plaie dou col	of the wound on the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound is on the neck and it is single, there is no difference between it and that of the head, except that the nerves or artery of the neck are cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is a nerve, there is nothing else to do but let the wound heal and not put anything constricting on it, because it hurts the nerves and makes them withdraw.Se c’est l’artere, si faut la cierer.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and not put anything cold on the wound, because the substance of the nerves is cold, and their continuations are with the brain, which is the highest member;Car la chaleur les meut et li sang est chaude.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but for medicine, as with clean chalk washed in sweet water and mixed with rose oil, and cooked washed also in sweet water,
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other mineral stones in this way, and moist ointments.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then cut it and bind it, then heal it until it is cured.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and she is pregnant and full of fluid, then pierce it or lower it;
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	and if the artery is cut, and bleeding ensues, then it should be stopped, and ligated, and cauterized if necessary;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	and if the spine of the throat is cut, or the windpipe, and the passage is guarded through which food travels,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	if one cuts above the cane of the throat, and does not touch the throat but resets it according to its natural shape;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then he stretches it gently, and leaves it for a few days, then he treats it with purifying ointments until it is healed;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound has left an impression on the bone, then he will;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are bone fragments, if you can pull them all out, and those that you cannot reach, then leave it until the wound heals.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	and let it heal and close up the wound.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	and if the wound is fresh, then powder it with the powder I have described.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and it has a fistula, then treat it as I said in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound from a spear or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a deep wound from a spear or knife, and the patient breathes with difficulty, then know that the wound is deadly;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not deep but fresh and bleeding profusely, do not apply the powder at first or ligature it for fear of causing fainting,
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and returns to health, and heals the illness;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but it applies an attractive ointment, and binds it .ij. times a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you don't have an ointment, put old cotton in the wound to soak up moisture,
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and let the patient sleep on the wound for 3 days, or 4, or more;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if there will come no spasms, nor trembling of the heart, nor twitches of the eyes;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see the good disposition, then you know that the wound is saved.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat it with poultices and other remedies until it is healed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	and if it cannot heal and keeps weeping, then you know that there is a fistula; treat it thus as it should be treated.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife incision, and it is simple, on the front or back, then the treatment of that which is in front.
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	if it is large, then stitching; and if it is small, then powder; and if it is deep in the bone, and has chipped off pieces, then want the wound, and draw out the foreign bodies if they are dislodged.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not dislodged, then let the wound fester, so that it will push out the foreign bodies.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds in other members is the judgment as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	of a rupture of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	There are great, medium, and small ruptures of the belly. The great one is when the intestines burst out of the abdomen, and they must be returned to their place as quickly as possible, and then the patient should lie on his back for four or five days, until the wound has healed. If it happens that he cannot bear to have them returned to their place, let him hold a heated iron against the rupture until he is able to endure having them put back in; otherwise, let him die. If this happens at night, the patient should be wrapped tightly around his waist with a cloth, and then the intestines can be pushed back in the next day. The medium one is when only the membrane bursts out, and it can be returned to its place without any difficulty. The small one is when only a little wind escapes.
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	from the great wound, except sometimes for the intestine or the nerve of the intestines, by which they enter.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	and the stitching is more difficult, and sometimes the small wound is worse than the great one.
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because one can no longer put the intestines back in if they are not gradually warmed.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	and when the intestines feel cold they contract at once and cannot be put back in.
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And so the wound heals more easily, because one puts the intestines back in their place little by little along with the others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And you should know that there are four types of hernia:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	the .ij. common sutures occur in the suture of the abdomen,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the suturing of other wounds on the body and .ij. other proper sutures are common to other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	and yet they are more appropriate with the suture of the abdomen, and I will say one and declare each one.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and some intestine is protruding,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and if it is difficult to reset, it can be done by one of two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or because the wound is small, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen due to coldness.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, warm it in such a way:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	soak a sponge or soft cloth in warm water
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	or you can boil in water squills and cypress and pepper,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and pluck the intestines until the swelling is removed;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and sometimes this wine-based remedy is made, and it helps to soothe and reduce swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling go down, then moisten the intestines with water or with a mixture of herbs that have been cooked.
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	for it is constipated and needs only a little to relieve it;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if he cannot pass anything, they make a small cut with an instrument used for hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first remedy is better than cutting,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	that one must not cut without great necessity;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the instrument for splitting it:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	cut inside the curve and not outside, and see the shape here:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines jump out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	then put it back according to its natural shape in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	if you have the power, for this is best.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is large and it is in the lower part of the belly,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	you should make the patient lie on his back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and puts his legs above his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it is in the lower part of the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	if he puts his head and feet higher than the parts below,
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and also if the rupture of the belly is in one of the .ii. parts
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	if you put your understanding into it so that the injured part is higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and thus one should manage what I say in large and small wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For small wounds, use what you are skilled at,
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	then have in your hand .i. minister pitous [a poultice] that covers the entire wound with its hand,
et assemble les levres;	and bring together the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common method of suturing,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you should thread a needle or multiple needles, depending on the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave about a finger's width from the edge of the wound, and insert a needle with a strong thread through it;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierces the .2. heads of the skin with the .2. heads of the syringe,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is under the skin inside, until you make it pierce that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and brings together the .2 heads of the syringe the .4 together;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then it pulls with a doubled thread around the needle of .2 parts,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then assemble the two parts of the wound smoothly,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave a space of two fingers and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie it to the thread as you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and do not stop doing this according to what you need of needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until the entire wound is restrained;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and let the needles be medium-sized, between thin and thick,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because thin needles pierce all the way through the flesh, and those that are too thick cannot pierce well:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	one must place the needles opposite to where the arrow came from; for it is not advisable to go too deep, or else one might break the limbs. That is why they should be medium-sized;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and one must not push the needles too deep into the flesh and through the skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	so that they do not cut and open the wound before it heals;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then cover the ends of the needles with wax or a similar substance so that they do not hurt the patient when they sleep,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and place towels or cloth on the ends of the needles to keep them in place,
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leave them until the wound is healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this method of sewing with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because it requires only one needle or at most two.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second sew is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and you shall sew together the two heads of the skin and the two heads of the syphac together on a needle with a strong thread;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have sewn these heads all four together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	then re-insert the needle into the part where you began, in the manner that one sews drapes;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and place a distance between each stitch of the thickness of a small finger;
ceste costure sevent li home,	this cloth seven men,
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sewed up a wound one man had in his belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	who had been stabbed with a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was more than a palm-width long,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and cut out the intestines, leaving them about two palms long.
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and stitch up the wound in the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I returned the intestines to their proper place after they had been out for twenty-four hours,
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	and the wound healed within fifteen days, and he recovered.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged him to have died, and this was a miracle.
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and I did not treat it with ointments, for I was in a place where there were no such things as ointments or medicines;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and I placed clean cotton on the wound twice a day and washed it with honey water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	Now, I will tell you about two proper methods of suturing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	take the needle, and pierce it through from outside to inside;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	when it has pierced through straight into the heart, then pull out the needle where you inserted it.
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and have her pierce from another spot inside out to the outside;
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and the understanding of this sewing is that you sew as the leatherworkers do with hides,
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and let the ointment remain on one side while you dress the other, until the stitch is completed all around.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of stitching, which Galen describes correctly,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	if it is like some people do, who unite the two parts naturally,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and they apply one of the cut heads to the other head, in such a way:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	stick a needle or sharp instrument close to the pain, and pierce only that spot
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	and leave the two gums of the ulcer
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the needle and pierce it from the outside just into the inside,
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	as the two gums of the ulcer
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then pierce both sides of the deflecting part to the inside, in two other small holes that are on the opposite side;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the usual and most common way to sew.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen says this, and some testify,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	that one should sew the belly with two needles, having thread in each;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one needle must be pushed from one side, and the other from the other, in the manner of those who sew sores;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	and know that when the hernia is in the abdomen,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	the incision must be made lower than other places in the abdomen.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgment of the wound is the same as the judgment of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it happens that when you find the fresh wound full of blood, as long as the fire has moved it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	then put back the intestine and the bowels; then place the cauterizing charcoal
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if the fire has moved it, then place some ointment on it while the wound is bleeding;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and tie the thread, and sew the edges of the wound, and the membrane;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then heal the wound as with the others until it is healed.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	and if you have no medicine, put on old cotton as soon as it starts to leak fluid,
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and change it twice a day until it is healed.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you do not need any other medicine for various wounds when they are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound affects the principal limbs,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	then you should moisten a light cloth in tempered oil, or rose oil,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it around the ankles and under the armpits;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	and if he feels pain or swelling in his bowels, and this happens frequently,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	if you enema with red wine, especially if the constipation reaches the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	and it pierces inside, and you will know that when it is the large intestine, it is easier to heal than the small intestine.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine which is called 'young' cannot heal when it is raw,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	and it is because of the thinness of their walls, and because of the subtlety of all the body, and the proximity of its nature to the nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the testicle pops out of the wound, put it back as far as the intestines, while it is fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	and if it has become old and turned green or black, then you should tie off the area that is black so that no blood flow comes from it,
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	because there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	then cut what is between the ligature,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and place the two fingers during the part below the wound to relieve the extraction when the sutures are cut and the wound is cleaned.
de la routure dou boueil	of the wound from the boiling
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are torn and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	one can restore it in some people,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I saw a man was wounded in the belly with a lance;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and it became a fistula and discharged fluids, and he experienced flatulence and winds;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treated him according to what I knew, and did not cease to apply poultices until he was healed and the wound closed.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw him sweating, I suspected that the patient had pain in his belly;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and he did not suffer any harm, but remained in good condition, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and some experimentalists say that when there is a minor wound in the intestine, it must be bound in such a way:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take fine thread from a large testicle, then bring together the lips of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the tremor has opened its mouth, it puts itself on top of both lips;
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	if it opens its mouth wide;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then it shakes its head, and this happens as long as it cannot get loose,
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then it has another tremor in the same way as before, until the wound is completely healed;
et cout la plaie.	and examine the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If they pierce the intestines and cause no harm to the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	one can sew up the intestine with a thin thread cut from the intestine of an animal,
en teil maniere:	in this way:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take the end of this intestine thread which is very charred,
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	and then tie to the end of this thread a thin twisted flax thread,
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	then thread the needle, and sew up the intestine, and return it to its socket;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	and this way of sewing up a hernia is not useless except according to the way of faith and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	and if the wound is great and wide, especially when it is in one of the small intestines, there is neither healing nor health without subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of fistula wherever it may be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that any wound or abscess, when it breaks open, is universally called a "fistula."
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	especially when it is lumpy and swollen.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And a fistula is according to the green [vein] a hardened, white node, where one does not feel pain,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and it is as thick as the feather of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	and sometimes it is clear and thin, and sometimes thick.
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes it is small, and sometimes large;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	and I have spoken of it in the section on wounds, that any wound which is not cleaned and has no scabs,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	this is only due to one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	that is, by the smallness of the blood or body;
ou por sa malice;	or because of its wickedness;
